Trump cards can be used to conquer other cards when no more cards of the same suit are there to offer. After each deal player have to make a \"Call\" or \"bid\" for the number of hands he/she can capture, and the objective is to capture at least that many hand in a round, and try to break other player i.e. stop them from getting their Call. The basic game strategy of Gin Rummy is to improve one's hand by forming melds and eliminating deadwood. Aces are considered low, they can form a set with another aces but only the low end of runs.
